# Return a full list of the names of B.C. Data Catalogue records

Return a full list of the names of B.C. Data Catalogue records

## Usage

``` r
bcdc_list()
```

## Value

A character vector of the names of B.C. Data Catalogue records

## Examples

``` r
# \donttest{
try(
  bcdc_list()
```
